thou ſhal haue cometh ſpecyal grace god viſiteth comyth god ſendeth ſuffreth al wyl good ſigne yt loueth therfore thanke god euer viſitacion beſeche hym euer mercy god knoweth entēt therfore dn̄a oculos ioſeph et ait veni dormi mecum ¶soo daye lady loked ioſeph toke hym mantel ſayd come ſlepe wyth aſſone ioſeph vnderſtode meanynge anone yede fledde waye lefte mantell thē ne woman cried xl dayes xl nyghtes wythoute mete drynke ¶thenne god gaue hym two table ſtone whiche god wrote wyth owne fyngres ten commaundementes toke theym moyſes ¶and bad hym teche hem people whan moyſes came downe peple face bryghte ſonne two ſpites ſtondyng hede lyke two horne ſoo people myght ſpeke wyth hym clerenes abſcondit moyſes faciem ſuā ¶thenne moyſes hyde face wyth kerchiff thenne one leef wryten thre cōmaundemētes longen god thoſe ben thyſe ¶the firſt thou ſhalt worſhippe thy god loue hym aboue thinge thou ſhall directe maner thynge goddis wyll byfore thyne owne ſue thyn owne wylle ¶the ſeconde cō maundemente thou ſhalt take name veyne ſaye thou ſhall bee called goddis childe cryſten man • fende thenne name vayn ¶alſo thou ſhall ſwere god noo parte body noo thynge made forderynge trouthe yet whan thou arte conſtreyned therto ¶the thirde commaundemente thou ſhall kepe thyne holy daye ſaye thou ſhall erly vp late downe ſerue god holy daye thou arte werkedaye thyne owne werke beſy ſhall thou hooly daye ſerue god ¶the fourthe commaundemente thou ſhall worſhippe thy fader thi moder yt brought worlde alſo thy godfader thy godmoder yt made cryſten man thy fader vnder god hath cure charge thy ſoule ¶the fyfthe thou ſhall ſle man nother wyth tonge wyth thy honde wyth euyll enſample ſixte thou ſhall ſtele mannes godes vii thou ſhalt doo lechery viii thou ſhall bere noo falſe wytneſſe nynthe thou ſhall nat coueyte thy nyghboures godes ne thing longeth ayenſt wyll tenthe thou ſhall nat deſire thy neyghboures wyf ne coū ſeyll noo waye euyll ſholde harme vilonye huſbonge thies x cōmaundmentes whiche euery criſten man woman bonde kepe thus moyſes figure token criſte moyſes camme bifore yaue lawe criſte came gaaf grace mercy ¶for ſame maner moyſes fette people oute egypte thrughe rede ſee forth hylle sinay ſame wyſe criſt whan came prechynge myracles doyng fette people derneſſe ſynne euyl lyuyng thorugh water baptyſme hylle vertuous lyuyng ¶and therfore wyll ſhryue hym clene leue fowle lyuing kepe commaundementis god made couenaunte kepe criſtning thēne ſhal encreaſed hygher thā ony hyl erth yt heuen wyll thus muſte fedde wyth fyue loues two fyſſhes ¶we rede daye holy chirche goſpell criſte fedde fyue thouſand people wyth fyue looues two fyſſhes fyrſte loff fyue contricion ſynne ſeconde ſhryfte mouth thirde ſatiſfaction treſpaſſe ¶the fourth tourne ayen ſynne ofte aferde ſhall doo well fyfthe perſeueraunce good lyuynge two fyſſhes ben good oryſons almeſdedes thyſe noryſſhed water wepynge teres deuocion thyſe two fyſſhes geten god wylle ¶narracio ¶it wreten ſomtyme man called pyers ryche man ſoo harde noo begger myght gete 〈◊〉 hym thenne • tyme happed ſo many beggers ſatte gyder place ſpake pyers myghte gete noo good hym ¶thenne ſpake one theym mayſter ſayde wylle ye ley wyth ſhall gete noo good hym soo made wager thenne wente man forth came pyers place ſet hym doune porche halle dore abode tyll pyers came anone ſawe pyers ſpake ſoo horryble pyers grete angre ſeruauntes came hym wyth baſket brede toke loof wyth myghte caſte atte beggers hede ſmote hym breſt ſayd ſtoppe thy mouth wyth deuylle ſtoppe anone begger caught loofe ranne waye felowes ſhewed loof ſoo gate wager ¶thenne next nyghte happed ſoo pyers ſhryuen brought bedde▪ ſoo deyed anone fendes came take ſoule thenne lady redy bad brynge ſowle ſoo dyde thenne noo thynge helpe ſoule lof caſt begger thenne ſayde fendys gaaf ayenſte wylle therfore ryght ſholde helpe hym ¶thenne wente oure lady ſone prayenge hym graunte ſoule goo body ayent loke yf ¶wolde amende 〈◊〉 thenne lorde badde vere ſoule ayen body whan ſoule wyth body anone ſatte vp gaaf great ſyghynge called hym ſeruauntes tolde hem hard dome dampned hadde lof caſt begger ¶therfore anone made ſelle good deled poure people fore goddis ſake whan hadde done ſoo made hym ſelfe heremyte holy man ¶here ye maye well wyte grete almeſdede preyers made man ſo preuy wyth god ſoo ſyker ayenſt dome ¶for haue done almyſdede goddis ſake ſhall bee ſaued yf oute dedely ſynne ¶we fynde vowtry man take another mannys wyfe woman another mā huſbonde greuous ſinne ye ſhall enſample ¶narracio ſomtyme man made charcoles wode whan made grete fyre leye therby nyght ſoo aboute mydnyght came woman rennynge afore man blacke horſe faſte myght ryde hunted abowte wyth naked ſwerde aboute fyre ſo laſt man ſlewe woman hew peces caſt fyre rode ayen wyth myght soo whan man ſawe done many nyghtes thenne went lord told hym mater thenne lorde bolde knyght ſai • wyte mente 〈…〉 thyder nyght fonde man peyne euerlaſtyng blyſſe god brynge v amen ¶dominica paſſione dnī good men wymmen daye called ſondaye paſſion weke daye oure lord iheſu criſte began paſſion 〈◊〉 iewes ſuche enuye • • cauſe tolde diſpyte repreef ¶narracio ¶we rede geſtes romaynes yt emperoure ſente grete man lō de iuge came ther man countre coude ſwere othe ye nay whan iuſtice came emong made peple ſwere bokes ſeſſiones gaue charge ſo people toke enſample iuſtice ſwere men dyd oure lordes paſſion ſydes armes nayles face woundes blood herte ſo forthe took ſo vſe cōmen people ſwoore dyd thenne day iuſtice ſat office paſſion openly hadde hanging vpon croce ſaynge conſummatum eſt endyd yt ſaye prophecy paſſion hath end wherfore clothes myn autre ben take away criſtes clothes wer take fro ſo doon naked croce ſaue vnder pounce pylate oure ſake olde ſawe yt foule begnnnynge hathe fowle endyng nowe ſee howe pylate began curſedly ended full wretchedly ſaynt auſtyn ſaith curſed lyuyng firſt aſketh curſyd ende forgeteth hym ſelf lyuyng full lyke forgete hym ſelfe laſt ende pylate knyghtes ſone called tyrus gate hym woman hyghte pyle womannys fader hyghte atte whan childe borne ſette moders name grande fader ſoo bothe name called hym pylat ¶thenne whan thre yeres age moder brought hym kynges courte thenne hadde knyghte another ſone nygh lyke pylates age knightes ſone rule gentyler manfully goodly beloued pylate ſoo hate enuye therof pylate • ſlewe knyghtes ſone thenne knyghte wonder ſory yet wolde ſlee pylate ſente hym rome hoſtage trybut knyght ſholde paye themperour ¶thenne happed kynge fraunce hadde ſent ſone theder ſame cauſe thenne cauſe ¶whan pylate ſawe beloued chereſhed therfore pylate ſlewe hym thē ne ſo curſed themperoure counſeyll romayns ſente pylate contree yt called pounce people contrey ſo curſed ſlewe ony come bee thyr mayſter ouer hem soo whan pylate come thyder applied hym maners ſoo wyth whyles ſotyltye ouercome hem mayſtrye gate name called pylate po •• ce • grete domynacion power thenne kynge iheruſalem ſent made lyeuftenaunt vnder hym londe iury pylate lyked well •• office preuely ſente themperour offyce confermed hym vnwetynge kynge herode kynge tyme wherfore whan kynge herode herde hadde done ſoo wrothe enmyes vnto tyme oure lorde iheſu criſt take thenne become frendis ayen fylle bothe one aſēt criſtis deth thenne happed afterward themperour fylle ſyke ſent criſte hele hym tolde hym cryſte heled tho euer wolde come hym maner ſykeneſſe ſoo euer ſykeneſſe ſoo bee thenne pylate done hym deth meſſager come thenne whan themperoure vnderſtode ſent pylate made hym come hym ¶and whan pylate herde ſore aferd take criſtis cote ſoo whan come rome themperour thoſe preſēce made pilate good chere whyle criſtis •• te themperour ſwore byfore ſhold ded thenne toke cote anone cote themperour ſore wrothe wythe pylate putte hym pryſō tyll take counſeyll dethe ſhold deye thenne ſoone pylate wiſt vnderſtod ſholde dede toke owne knyfe ſlewe hym ſelf wyth whan emperour herde therof vnderſtode ſleyn hym ſelf thenne anone made bynde grete ſtone aboute pylats necke caſte hym water called tyber thenne whan caſt therin fendes made ſuche noyſe cite rome ſore afreyd ¶thenne whan emperour ſawe made take hym vp agayn thenne caſte water betwyx two hie hilles ſoo longe tyme water many horryble ſyghtes ſeen aboute curſed man thus oure lorde iheſu cryſte wymmen cyte whan ſee hym ſoo fowle fayre wyth lougged drawe pyte wepte vpon hym ¶thenne ſayde lord hem nolite flere ſuper ſed ſuper vos et filios veſtros ¶ye wymmen iheruſalem wepe ye vpon children· ¶narracio ¶we rede clerke gretly lerned dyuinyte whiche ſtodyeth beſely haue broughte boke god wolde byleued one god • thre perſones • ſoo walked day ſtodyeng mater ſee ſonde ware faire child ſittyng ſee ſonde lytyl ſhelle honde therwyth toke water ſee caſt al • tyl pytte faſt thenne ſayd mayſter chyld sone •• dooſt thou ſayd syre abowte haue water y• ſee lytyll pytte thē ne ſaid mayſter ſhalt rede ther iewe wente criſten man felowe churche criſten people herde maſſe et poſt miſſam dixit iudeus maſſe ſayde iewe thus si ego tantum ediſſem quātū comediſti non eſuriem vt puto tribus diebus ¶if hadde eten aſmoche thou haſte eten ſholde nat hungred trowe thre day ſaid criſten man iewe vere nichil comedi forſothe ſaide criſten man iewe ete maner mete daye thē ne ſaide iewe ego vidi te god ſhewe ſome myracle womannys helpe whanne hadde prayed longe gregory went autre ayen founde thoſte turnyd rede fleſſhe bloode bledynge ſhewyd woman thenne ſhe cryed ſayd nowe lorde crye mercy byleue thou art god man goddes ſone heuyn fourme brede thenne badde gregory people pray agayn ſholde turne ayen bredes lykeneſſe dyd ſame ofte houſled woman lacyua ¶and therfore lete v doo worſhyp yt may ſacramēte nat myſbeleue ¶alſo fynde deuonſhyre beſide exbridge woman ley ſeke nygh dede ſente holy perſone aboute mydnyght haue rightes thenne man haſte myght aroſe went churche toke goddes body boxe yuery put boſome went forth toward womā went foreſte fayre mede next way happed boxe fell oute boſome grounde wente forth wyſt nat cāme woman herde confeſſion aſked ſhe wold houſted ſhe ſaid ye ſyre thēne put hōde boſom ſought boxe whā founde full ſory ſadde ſayd dame wyl goo goddis body come anone ayen ſoo went forth ſore wepynge ſympleneſſe ſoo com welow tree made ther rode ſtryped hym ſelf naked bete hym ſelf blode ranne doune ſydes ſaid thus hym ſelf thou ſymple man haſt thou loſte thy lord god thy maker thy ſaucour creature whan thus beten ſelf dyd clothes wente forth thenne ware py • ar fyre laſted erthe •• uen aſtonyed therof •• bleſſed hym wente therto lay ſacrament fallen oute boxe graſſe pylour ſhone bryght ony ſonne laſted goddis body heuen • eſtis foreſte come aboute goddis body ſtode compaſſe rounde aboute kneled iiii knee ſaue blacke horſe kneled one knee thenne ſaide yf thou ony beſt may ſpeke charge goddis name preſent fourme brede tel thou kneleſt thy one knee thenne ſaid fende helle wyll knele myghte made ayenſt wyll writon euery knelyng heuen erthe ſhall worſhyp lord god art thou lyke horſe ſaid make people ſtele ſuche towne hāged ſuche toune nother thenne ſayd holy perſon commaunde goddis fleſſhe blode yt thou goo wylderneſſe thou ſhalt neuer dyſeaſe cryſten people anone wente waye myght noo lenger abyde thēne man went forth woman dyde ryghtes whiche ſhe ſaued went euerlaſtyng ſaluacion whiche brynge v v ſhed blode vpon rode tree amen de feſto ſcī andree appoſtoli good men wymmen ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaynt andrewis daye ye ſhall faſt euen come god al holy chirche worſhip holy ſaynt daye iii ſpecyall vertues one greate holyneſſe doynge ſeconde good lyuyng thirde greate paſſyon ſuffryng ¶he man holy lyuyng whan vnderſtode herde ſaynt iohan baptiſt preching deſerte anone lefte worldly occupacion wente hym diciple ſoo daye cryſt come walkynge way ſaint iohā baptiſt ſawe hym walking ſaid diſciyples ecce agnus dei qui tollit peccata mundi ¶see lambe god ſhal awaye ſynne al worlde whan saynt andrewe herde anone leete ſaynt iohan baptiſte ſewed criſte whanne herde criſte preche pleaſed ſo well anon wēt fett petyr broder cryſte preche thenne caſte grete loue god ſone wer ſee galile fiſſhinge criſte cāme called anon left fyſſhī ge ſhyppe nette ſued criſt euir wyth tyll ſtyed vp heuyn ¶narracio ¶thenne ſaint andrewe prechyd amonge people day prechyd happed ſoo man emong peple called nycoll hadde lyued many wynters lechery yet grace god thoughte amende lyue whanne herde word god ſo grete vertue ſholde putte awaye temptaciones ſynne lete write goſpell bare wherſoeuir wēt vertue therof abſteyned ſelue fro ſynne yet daye tēptacion fende forgate ſelf went agayn brodellys houſe vſed bifore whā cāme thidre wymen lokyd vpon cryed oute ſayde thou old ſely man doſt thou go home ayen ſe ſoo many maruayles maye nat haue doo thenne nycoll bethought goſpell vpon anoon went ſaint andrewe tolde caas prayed ſainte andrewe pray ſoule might ſauyd thenne ſaint andrewe wolde neuir ete drynke tyll wyſte whether nicoll ſholde ſauyd ſaint andrewe faſtyd fyue day brede water praied beſily night day thenne cāme voyce ſayd thou haſte faſtyd prayed make nycol ſame thenne ſhalbe ſaued thēne ſaint andrewe bad nycol faſte fyue day brede water praye beſily vnto god ſo dyd thenne come voyce ſaint andrewe agayn ſayd thy prayer thy faſtinge hath made nycoll yt loſte founde ayen ſhalbe ſaued ¶narracio ¶alſo nother myracle 〈…〉 yonge man come ſainte andrewe tyme ſaide priuely sir modre hath longe aboute • ſholde lye wold nat doo wyll ſhe hath accuſed buſſhop ſay •• wolde haue doon ſinfull dede wherfore wote well ſhall dede yet hadde leuyt dye • e ſclaundre modre ſo foule therfore beſeke pray may take deth paciētly ſaluacion ſoule thenne ſayd ſainte andrewe go forth thy dome ſhal go ſo therwith peple come fe • e bifore buſſhoppe whanne modre accuſed hym ſaide noo thinge helde peas▪ thenne ſaide ſaint andrewe innocēs ſāguis enis ſure cauſa dampnabitur curſed woman luſt body wrongfully aboute dampne childe deth vengeaunce wil come thenne ſayd ſhe loo ſyre iuſtice euer ſyth myght haue wyll hathe drawen man counſeyll • ſocour thenne iuſtyce commaunded caſt yonge man water drowne hym put ſaint andrewe pryſon tyll aduyſed deth ſholde deye thenne ſaynt andrew prayed beſely vnto god helpe ſocour thenne anone come grete thondre made people ſo aferde feyne fette ſaynt andrewe oute pryſon euyn therwyth come lyghtenyng fyre brenned moder yonge man ſyght people ¶and thus man ſaued iuſtice grete myracle tourned criſten feyth moche people wyth euer belyued god ſaynte andrewe therby ye may ſee holy lyuyng alſo gret miracle wyrchyng oon day went ſee ſyde ſaw drowned man caſte oute water thēne andrewe prayed god rere hym ayen lyfe anone man roſe thenne andrew aſked hym drowned ſayd x men gyder herde holy man hyght andrew commyng preching ſee come gret tempeſt drowned v gyder wolde god caſt londe togyder myght haue reyſed lyfe gyder ayen thenne ſaynt andrewe prayed god al bodyes myghte come togyder ſoo dyde caſt vp dyuerſe contreys thenne ſaynt andrewe made ordeyned gader theym gyder thenne kneled downe prayed god longe theym tyll reyſed lyfe thenne ſaint andrewe made knele doune thanked god preched taught theym cryſten feyth cryſtened theym whan ſtedfaſte feith ſent home owne countrey wyth moche ioye theym many myracles dyde longe tel thus ye maye ſee myghty myracles werkynge reyſed ſoo many men lyfe alſo ſuffred grete paſſion criſtis ſake whan cyte pateas tourned feyth wyfe egeas egeas grete man made moche people doo ſacrifyce offryng mawmentis ſaint andrewe repreued hym therof anone made take hym wolde haue made hym doo ſacryfyce wolde ſtedfaſtely bode ayenſte hym preued many enſamples cauſe people ſholde worſhyppe god fendes helle thenne egeas wode wrothe made men take andrewe ſtrype hym naked bete hym ſcourges yt al body ranne blode ¶and thenne made bynde hym honde fote made doo ¶on croſſe ſhold peyne theron longe deyed whan andrewe come place cro kneled doune ſaid thus salue crux qui corpore criſti dedicata e holy thou croſſe arte halowed made holy precious body lord iheſu criſte deſyre clyppe wherfore take yelde mayſter iheſu criſte dyed croſſe thenne andrewe ſtode vp dyde clothes gaue tourmentours bad theym doo charged doo iuſtice thenne bounde hym croſſe honde fote hede downewardis ſtreyned hym soo blode braſt oute atte euery knot rope ſoo henge thre dayes alyue prechyng people ſoo come prechynge many thouſandes people· pyte yt hadde hym bad egeas myght take doune croſſe wyll deye euyn therwith hiis enim dictis ſplendor niuis circuiens eum quaſi per mediam horam grete lyghte come aboute hym noo man myght ſee hym ſpace halfe houre thenne ſayd ¶narracio ¶there nother riche man prayer ſaint nycholas childe made fair chapel worſhippe god ſainte nycholas hapned day child taken enmyes ladde another ſtraunge countre ther ſeruyce kinges courte happed ſaint nycholas day bethoughte greate myrthe ſolempnite made day faders chapel home heuy ſighed full ſore thenne king herde therof thenne ſayd kynge nicholas menyſt thou ſigh ſo ſore mery thou muſt nedes abyde v anon cāme greate wynde ſmote houſe braſte childe • aughte vp cuppe bare 〈◊〉 honde ſet bifore ga •• chapell fader made feſt thenne made grete ioye mirthe myracle lo thus ye maye ſee howe grete compaſſion ſainte nicholas hadde miſcheef diſeaſe ſome bokes ſay childe normandye taken ſowdā beyonde ſee ofte beten one whāne beten ſainte nicholas daye putte pryſon thenne wepte ſore hee fyll aſlepe whanne awoke faders churche ¶de concepcione beate marie virginis goode men wymen ſuche daye ye ſhall haue concepcion oure lady whiche day feſte holy churche maketh mynde mē cion conception oure lady thre ſpeciall cauſes firſte fader holyneſſe ſecounde moders godneſſe thrid mekeneſſe hadde fader called ioachim ſo holy man whan xv yere age departed godes thre partes one parte dealed wydowes faderleſſe child ſecounde parte gaue pore nedy thridde parte kepte ſelue houſeholde whan xxxii yere age grete godeneſſe anne weddyd whan wedded gydder xxii yere whiche tyme anne neuir diſpleaſed maner thinge nother night daye ſhe ſo gentyll bothe good holy yet god ſente theym frute body barr • yn wherfore made vowe god wolde ſende theim childe wold offre vnto vp temple ſerue god nyghte daye ¶thenne daye ioachim wente nyghboures temple doo offrynges buſſhop highte iſachar rebuked openly bifore people ſaid ioachym falleth nat art barrayne haſt frute offrī ge people god hath ſē te frute ieruſalem thenne ioachim ſore diſmayde aſtonyed rebuke thenne went hoome wepynge tooke ſhepeherd preuely ſhepe wente forth ferre countrey amonge monteyns hylles purpoſed haue ben lyf neuir cō home anne wyf ¶than whanne ioachim gon anne ſory prayed god ſaid lorde woo barreyne may haue frute nowe ouir huſbonde gone away know nat whether gone lorde haue mercy thēne ſhe prayed thus aungell cōme doune comforted ſaide anne good comforte thou ſhalt haue childe thyn olde age neuir noon ſuche ne neuir ſhalbe ¶thenne anne aferd angellys wordes ſight hym laye alwaye prayer ſhe hadde dede thenne went ſame aungell ioachim ſaide theſe wordes badde ioachim take lambe offre ſacrifice god ſoo dyd whan ſo fro mydday euenſong tyme ley grō de prayer thankynge god al hert thēne morow aungell badde wente homwarde anne wyf ſhepe whan cāme nygh home aungell cāme anne badde goo yate called golden yate abyde huſbonde tyll cōme thenne ſhe glad toke 〈◊〉 maydynes went gate ſhe mette ioachim ſaid lord thanke wedowe wyf barrayn nowe ſhall bere childe wo wepinge nowe ſhall ioye likynge ſoone anne conceyued oure lady whan ſhe borne ſhe called mary aū gell badde bifore thanne yt ſhe wenyd ſhe brought tē ple lefte emong virgynes ſerue god bothe nyght day thenne ſhe ſo meke emonge virgynes lyuynge virgynes called quene virgynes soo ſhe mekeſt al ſaintes heuyn mooſt redyeſt helpe theym call nede ¶narracio ¶we rede holy wrytte myracle oure lady lordes man yt hadde gadred moche good lordes 〈◊〉 gadred went bere lothe thenne ther theuys ſette robbe hym▪ waye wode muſte nedes goo soo whanne come wode bethoughte hym yt hadde ſaide lady ſaulter wonte knelyd doune began ſaye come lady lyke fair mayden ſet garlonde hede eche aue maria ſhe ſette roſe garlond ſoo brighte woode ſhone therof whan done kyſſed erthe wente waye thenne come theues toke hym ladde hym mayſter whiche ſeen thyſe doynges thenne ſayd hym woman yt ſet garlonde hede ſayd ſyre ſothe ſee ne woman ne garlonde thenne ſayde mayſter thefe wote well thou arte lordys man haſt moche good wyth wolde fayn wyte womā come thou kneleſt downe ſayd whā ſee aferde alſo bethoughte hadde ſayde oure lady faulter kneled doune ſay prayng lady helpe nede thenne ſayd loue goo thy waye praye v ſoo went waye ſauf founde helpe ſocour dere lady ¶but ye ſhall feſt firſt founde kynge englonde hyght wyllyam conquerour ſente thabbot ramſey kynge denmarke meſſage whan come ſee come tempeſt derkeneſſe wyth hym wende haue drowned euery man prayed beſely vnto god lady ſocour helpe dyuerſe ſayntes abbot pr • yed god lady full deuoutly thenne come theym fayr woman ſayd theym yf ye wyl haue concepciō lady worſhyp ii daye ſaynt nycolas day ſhe wyll redy helpe • ſocour tyme thenne abbot ſayd ye wyth good wyll wyſt ſhold ſeruyce feſt thenne ſayde ſhe ſame natiuyte • au • torne natyuite concepcion thabbot ſaid ſhold done full good wyll thenne anone tē peſte ceaſed well ſayled forth thabbot dyd meſſage come ayen ſauf ſoū de ſpedde well euery degre whan come home tolde kyng viſion kyng made hym preche reame aboute thus alowed holy chirche ¶narracio alſo fynde ſeculer chanon tyme wente ouer water haue doo avowtry wyth woman aboute begynne ſaye oure lady • yns inuytatory aue maria ther wyth fende caſte hym downe drowned hym wolde haue hym helle thenne come lady ſayd haſt thou take man fende ſayde fynde hym ſeruyce goyng avowtry thenne ſayd lady ſeruice anone reſtored hym lyf ayen bad hym ſynne bad hym halow concepcion ſoo dyde good man euer lyf ¶narracio ¶alſo clerke euery day vſed ſay ſeruice lady hapned counſeyll hys frendes ſholde haue wyf whan ſhulde ben weddyd bethoughte hadde nat ſaide oure lady ſeruyce thenne made peple go oute churche ſayd ſeruyce thēne knelyd doune ſaide ſeruyce tyll cāme antem oure lady quam pulcra e amica mea thenne oure lady apperyd vnto hym ſaide ſayſte thou faire honeſt wyll thou leue take nother thenne ſaide vnto oure lady wylte thou ſhall doo thenne ſaide lady thou wylt leue thy fleſſhly wyf ſerue ſone ſhall thy ſpouſe thou ſhalte haue crowne euirlaſtinge lyf kingdome heuyn whiche god bleſſed modre ſainte mary holy ſaintes heuyn brynge v al dre nowe euir amen sequitur ſermo breuis de ſancto thoma goode men wymen ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaint thomas day criſtes appoſtel ye ſhall faſte euyn worſhippe ſpecially thre cauſes firſte preuynge oure byleue grete woundres waye grete miracle day holy appoſtyll preuyd ſo oure faythe yt lefte trouble whan diſcyples ſaide yt lord ryſen fro dethe lyue haue ſeen ſpoke thomas ſaid wolde nat byleue tyll hadde pull honde ſide wound ſpere hadde made thenne viii day whan diſciples giddre thomas thē ne oure lorde ieſu criſte come bodily theym ſaide pay vobis pea thanne oure lorde ſayde thomas ynde mitte manū tuā latus men̄ putte thy honde ſyde wounde made ſpere ſmote herte et noli eſſe meredulus lengre beleue ſtedfaſte fayth thē ne whan thomas hadde doon ſo anone cryed ſayd grete wondre dominus meus et deus meus lorde god beleue yt thou arte god man lorde ſaide thus btī qui crediderūt nō viderūt bleſſed beleue ſe nat thou haſte ſeen thou byleueſte yet taryenge thomas brought v fadder beleue bleſſinge oure ieſu criſte ſpeketh ſainte gregory ſayth thomas ynde thou haſte holpe fayth woldeſt nat beleue tyll thou haddeſt felyd woundes thenne mary mawdeleyn dyd beleue firſte ſighte minus eſt enim maria magdalena que cicius credidit quā thomas qui diu dubitauit thus thomas preuyd oure feyth beleue nede neuir varye ne doubte ¶alſo thomas dyd deth lyf tolde kynge y• ſeen pal • yſe paradyſe many merueylles grete wondres dayes ¶narracio hit happed kynge ynde ſende meſſenger abbanꝰ indie requirēs artificē ſeke ſome crafty men contrey ceſar ſeke carpēter yt coude make hym palays pleſaunce thenne lorde ihū criſte met wyth abbanus ſente wyth hym thomas ynde alſo whan thomas abbanus paſſed ſee com cyte kyngis doughter wedded ſame daye wherfore maner peple commaunded mete amonge al people thomas abbanus come ſet mete thomas ete thoughte euere god luſte ete thenne come boteler thomas ſmote thomas cheke badde hym ete thenne ſayd thomas hym non hunc ſurgam donec manus que percuſſit canibꝰ aufertur ſhall ryſe place tyll ye honde yt ſmote brought wyth dogge thenne anone boteler went water lion met hym ſlew hym dranke blode ete body thenne come blacke dogge caught honde ſmote thomas brought hall ſyghte people layd downe byfore thomas thenne woman vnderſtode thomas wordes anone • neled dow • ne thomas cryed ſaid tho • arte god elles one diſciples ryght thou wylt ſoo thē ne kynge prayed thomas bleſſe doughter huſbande thē ne thomas glad therof ¶cepit ergo predicare beatus thomas therfore bleſſed thomas began preche tolde lord iheſu criſt yt tourned man wedded ſame daye wyff none made hym biſſhop ſame cite wyff anon martirs cryſtis ſake thēne wente thomas forth ynde kynge make hym paleys pleſaunce soo whan thomas come kynge gladde ¶and delyuered thomas grete ſōme gold make palays wyth thenne rode king forth meane tyme whan thomas ſholde haue made paleyſe hym thought better make paleyſe heuen erthe deled golde amō ge poure peple conuerted feyth thenne come kynge home went paleyſe redy whan herde thomas abbanus done wold haue put deth happed owne brother dede ſame time ¶and therfore putte theym bothe pryſon tyme buryed brother ¶thenne god wold whan brother laye longe dede roſe thomas made hym prayed kynge myghte haue wolde gyue hym moche gold toke thomas thēne kinge toke coūſeyl ſaid nay wil haue ſelf lete hym make another broder ſeen paleyce paradyſe made wyth gold arayed wyth precyous ſtones clothe golde ¶thenne kynge toke cryſtendome many thouſande wyth hym whan byſſhop ſaw kynge ſoo moche peple forſoke lawes tourned criſtendome ſore wrothe wyth thomas one theym ſayde wolde venge god wyth ſpere ſmote thomas thorugh body ſlewe hym thenne criſten peple buryed hym tombe cryſtall god wrought many myracles hym honde cryſtis ſyde wold neuer come tombe euer laye wythout alſo prechyng techyng taught duodecim gradus virtutum aſſignare primus eſt vt deum crederent qui eſt vnus eſſencia et trinus perſonis dedit eis triplex exemplum ſenſibile quomodo ſint diuidenci vna tres perſone primum ē quia vnum eſt homine ſapiencia et de vna procedit intellectus memoria et genium memoria eſt vt non obliuiſcaris intellectum vt intelligas que oſtendi poſſunt veldoceri ingenium ē vt quod didiceris inuenias secundum eſt quia vna vinea tria ſunt lignum folium et fructus et hec omnia tria ſunt vinea tercium ē quia capud noſtrum e • quatuor ſenſibus conſtat vno autem capite ſunt viſus auditus adoratus et guſtus et hec plura ſunt et tamen vnum capud secundus gradus eſt vt baptiſmum ſuſcipiat tercius gradus eſt vt fornicatione abſtineat quartus vt ſe ab auaricia tē peret quintus vt gulā diſtringeret sextus vt penitenciā teneret septiꝰ vt hiis perſeuerarēt octauus vt hoſpitalitatem marent nonus vt voluntatē •• e crowne golde ¶and whan syble ſhewyd emperoure ſhe ſaide 〈◊〉 him▪ childe ſhalbe greter thou arte euir euir ſhalbe therfore worſhip reuerēce thē ne anoon emperoure tooke enſence dyd worſhippe charged people doo ſame call childe god man thus criſten people may lerne worſhippe •• ruy • e childe day therfor • thridde maſſe daye ſaide myddaye tokenyng criſten peple ſhuld cōme offre worſhippe epularis come welbeloued derlinge tyme yt thou come ete wyth thy bredern borde feſte ¶thenne iohan roſe vp anone wolde haue gone forth wyth hym thēne ſaid lord vp ſōday thou ſhalt wyth thenne ſō day paſſyng feble die dominica conuenit ad iohannem vniuerſa multitudo populi soo ſonday come iohan grete multytude people thenne iohan made hem lede hym chirche might ſpeke ſaid hem yt ledde hem thus fide ſitis ſtabiles et man datis dei feruentes ye ſtable ſadde feyth feruent commaundementis god thenne ſayd one theym ſaye ye thus ofte v thenne ſayde yf ye loue gyder parfyghte charyte ſted faſt feythe ynought ſaluacion therfore ye ſtable feyth feruēt commaundementes god thenne commaunded make hym graue fore aulter whan made wente thē ne come ſuche lyghte aboute hym grete whyle noo man myghte ſee hym whan lyght gone graue full manna welled vp dothe ſonde water thus departed worlde blyſſe heuen neuer ſhall haue ende blyſſe brynge v deyed rode tree mankynde amen ¶sanctorum innocencium good frendis ſuche daye called innocentes daye ſome people calle childermas day child ſlayn day criſtis ſake called innocentes ſay wythout ſynne dyde noo ſynne god euer gretely greued wyth ſynne eſpecyal proude people ayenſt neyghbour • doyng hem wrong thyſe innocentes dyde neuer ſynne ne conſentyng ſinne wherfore may wel ſaye lyued wythout ſhame deyed wythout blame cryſtened owne blode home ſome moders armes holy chirche daye ſingeth redeth worſhip thyſe innocentes two yere age therfore aſhamed owne ſha •• defowled wyth maner ſpotte ſynne ſynne drawte kynd fader adam eue adam • eue ware ſame wiſe paradyſe ſtate innocen • naked ſhamed ſhappe al whyle wythout ſinne whan ſinned ſaw owne ſhappe ſhamed therof couered ſhap wyth leuys fygge tree ryght ſoo whan ſynne begynneth take • • e chylde thenne innocency goth away fro hym knoweth good •• le ylle good leueth good doth euyll thenne ſynneth thenne innocente noo lenger thenne greueth god thyſe chyldren lyued ſo longe knowe one ſleyne wythin age innocency wherfore lyued lyfe wythout ſhame blame kyng herode kynge iewes made ſlee hem wythoute gyfte whā thre kynges come kynge herode ſaid hym vbi ē qui natꝰ ē rex iudeorum ¶where borne kynge iewes bad hym telle come worſhyp hym ferre oute eſt thenne kynge herode foule aſtonyed wordis aſked clerkis childe ſholde borne ſayd bethelem iude thenne kynge herode tolde hem ſo bad hem goo thider worſhyp come ayen may goo worſhip hym alſo ſo kyngis wente thyder worſhypped cryſte whan hadde doone offryngis cryſte per aliam viam reuerſi ſunt ī regionem ſuam another waye tourned home ayen angel bad hem ſoo ſlepe thenne kynge herode wonder wrothe anone ordeyned ſle criſt whan made redy therto happed ſoo emperour rome ſente hym come hym haſt myghte two owne ſones accuſed hym emperour treſon thenne herode lefte purpoſe criſt tyme rode rome better ſones come home ayen wyth worſhip tofore yet alway thought ſle criſte leſte criſt come mannis eſtate wold haue put hym oute kyngdom thenne ſente anone bad hem ſlee child bethelem countrey aboute wyth two yeres age born ſame day ſo dyde kynge herode goyng comynge ſoo taryeng two yeres therfore made ſle euer wythin two yere age ſoo vengable party felle hym ſelf child ſlayn amonge ſame tyme come angell ioſeph ſaid hym accipe puerum et matrem eiꝰ et fuge egiptum take child moder flee egypte ſo dyde thus innocentes ſlayn wythout blame ſhamed theyr owne ſhappe criſtened home theyr blode fonte therfore ye ſhall vnderſtonde thre manere cryſtenyng one water criſtened fonte nother thyſe child criſtened owne blod thouſand marters moo ſhed blode cryſtis ſake thyrde cryſtenynge feyth whiche patriarkes prophetes holy faders byfore incarnacion lord iheſu cryſte byleued verely comynge cryſt· cryſtened feyth thus ye may ſee enmyte tyraunt kyng herode ſhede ſoo many childerns blode criſtis ſake treſpaſſed hym none wepte many mode • theyr hadde thomas alſo ſe • arraye alſo reuy •• yt thomas houſeholde▪ ſpake ſo moche people worſhippe thomas truer alſo bettre loue thenne bitwene kinge thomas laſte neuir bitwene two men wherfore putte enſample hapned fyll colde wynter kinge thomas come ryding gydder chepe ſide london kinge ware poure man well nere naked hadde clothes ſore colde thenne ſaide kinge thomas grete almes dede gyue pore man better clothes sir ſaide thomas ſuche ye ſholde take hede thenne hadde thomas cloke good ſcarlett well furred riche furre thēne kinge layd honde cloke wold haue pulled thomas haue gyue pore man thomas held faſte thus wraſtled long ſomoche like fall grounde laſt fauour thomas ſuffred kinge take cloke thenne kinge caſte pore man badde renne awaye faſte ſell bye thou beſette well thou maiſte fare bettre euir whyle thou leuyſt thenne thomas faynyd hym ſelue wrothe herte well pleaſed robe ſo wele beſette thenne people marueiled gretely firſt bitwene kinge thomas whan ſaw menyd people glade grete ſpotte therof ¶this ſay ſhewe enſample well louyd giddre thus thomas ſeruyd kinge manfully alſo muſt lerne oure olde patrone ſaint thomas ſerue god deuoutly ſeruyd god full deuotly aſſone made arſhcbiſſhop counterbury anone turnyd lyuynge bettre lyuynge thoughte ſerue kinge heuyn aſwell o king worlde bifore thenne anon layde awaye ſcarlet riche furres weryd clothe myddell pryce caſte awaye ſilke ſandyll weryd • ere next body right harde breche ſame whiche ſo moche vermyn horrible ſight ſee knewe fewe people alſo euery weneſday fryday made confeſſoure bete rodde vpon ba • e body like childe bete ſcole alſo waſſed euery day thre pore mennys foot knelinge croces way • aferd therof turned homwarde ayen yet morowe went agayn croſſes full blode thenne fledde homwardes agayn echone yet wolde nat leue therby went ayen thridde day fyre roſe oute erthe brent tonne hote feruent oyll cloſed therin put vndre fyre haue brente therin goddes owne derlynge kept ſo harme part body thenne whanche peple nyd dede vncloſed tonne found hole founde party bodye clothes thyng hadde touched therfore criſten people lete make churche worſhip god martirdome ſuffred ther emperour might nat ouircōme waye martirdome penaunce exiled yle called pathmos herd ſaint iohns modre ſone ſent rome dede gret ſorow cōpaſſion ſhe went rome whan ſhe herde exiled ſhe turned ayen went homwarde ſo whan ſhe came cyte called vetulam ther ſhe fyll ſeke dyed ſhe buryed beſide cyte roche whan ſhe hadde layne many yeres ſaint iames ſonne came thydre toke moders body ſmelled ſwete ſpycerye brought cyte buryed grete worſhip honoure de ſancto iohē baptiſta goode frendes ſuche daye ye iohn people waked home made thre maner fyres oone clene bone noo wode yt called bone fyre nother clene wode bone called wode fyre people ſytte wake therby thridde made wode bone yt called ſaynt iohnes baptyſed criſt whan baptyſed ecce aperti ſunt celi heuen opened et vidit ſpiritum dei deſcentē ſicut columba ſawe holy gooſt come downe doue et vox de celo dicens voys heuen ſpake thus ecce filius hym pryſon ordeyned bitwene wyf iohn might dede oute troublyng people comen people loued iohn well thenne herode ordeyned make grete feſte ſtates countre ſhulde holde peple ryſen ſo whan daye com feſte ſhulde holde al people ſeruyd mete herodes wyf couenaunt bitwene theim tho ſent doughter hall daunce tomble afore geſtes pleaſed fader ſo well ſwore grete othe ſaide pete quod vi dabo tibi aſk thou wylt ſhal gyue thenne modre bad ſaye ſhe ſaide caput iohannis baptiſte hede iohn baptyſt herode fayned wrothe ſory hadde made ſuche othe glad hert thenne ſēt pryſon ſmyte iohnes hede withoute wyndow theym wynde hopynge yt ſhuld neuer ryſe ayen lyf ¶thus ye may vnderſtonde holy yt man thenne aungell come fro heuyn tolde zacary conceyuig halowed moders wō oure lady toke therth byrthe aungell brought name fro heuyn criſte nyd oure lorde ieſu criſte holy man ¶ye ſhall vnderſtonde tha • ſainte iohn euangelyſt dyed ſame daye holy churche maketh noo mencion therof day holde criſtmas appered louers bad theym leue ther diſputacion well accorded heuyn made ſtryf thenne morow bifore al people either tolde viſion come theym diſpute ¶and thenne people thanked god almyghty bothe ſaint iohns faire miracle ¶alſoo two meſelles louyd wele thies two iohnes ſo cōmynge ſpake theſe two ſaintes whiche greteſt heuē ſoo one ſaide one greter thanne ſo begannne fyghte thenne come voys fro heuen ſayd fyghte heuen therfore fighte ye erthe v ben pea ſo ye therwyth bothe hole ſykeneſſe thanked god bothe ſaynt iohannis afterwarde holy men ¶and therfore lete v worſhyppe thyſe holy ſayntes· yt maye praye v may come euerlaſtynge bliſſe ¶sctōrum petri pauli good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue feſte ſaynt peter poule ye ſhall faſte euyn morowe come vnto chirche worſhyp god praye thyſe ¶ye ſhall vnderſtonde yt thyſe two appoſtles firſt grete ſynners left ſynne ſory contryte ſynned nomore lord toke hem enſample wyl leue ſynne ſhal ſaued ſhreuen forſaketh ſynne mercy foloweth yt doo vnderſtonde ye poule firſt ſoo hye ſoo feerſe ayenſt al goddis ſeruaūtes yt durſt precher deale wyth hym lefte grete malice ferſe gracious hye proud herte meke lowly goddis ſeruaūtes peter alſo held hym ſelf moſt perfyte ſtedfaſt criſtis dyſcyples wherfore made boſt vayn glory redy goo dethe wyth cryſt ſayd thus behoueth deye wyth the· whan cryſte ſey diſcyples ſhold forſake hym peter grete boſt forſoke criſt whan herde kocke crowe thenne remembred lord ſayd hym kocke crewe iii thou ſhalte forſake thenne peter went forth et fleuit amare wept bytterly hyd hym caue durſt come among bredren ſtone engliſſhe thou layeſt ſtone thou ſhalt fynde soo peter ſoo ſtedfaſt nether wele woo neuer flitered euer ſtode ſtedfaſt criſtis lawe euer ſynne mynde amende amyſſe afterwarde grete abſtynence ete ſuche inſtrumentis wroughte wyth lyues anone droue awaye enemyes whan ſawe cryed god mercy man euer prayed dede almeſdedes theym peine thus ye may well proue deuoute prayer helpen maye ſoule yt ben purgatory alſo almeſdedes helpen many ſoule sicut aqua extinguit ignem ita elemoſina extinguit pctm̄ ¶right water quencheth fyre ſoo almeſdede quencheth ſynne yt brenneth purgatory yf ben good lyff parfyghte charyte done yf almeſſe dede done ben ioye haue nede therto put treſour holy chirche goddes wyll ſoo deled releueth theym haue moſt nede therto ſo god aſſygneth thenne ſoules ben holpē therwyth thanke ſoule done thus ye may knowe well almeſdedes helpen gretly ſoules done fore ben purgatory ofte holy men haue herde fendes crye▪ make grete ſorowe wyth almeſdedes ſoules taken ¶narracio ¶we rede olde tyme gode peple wolde halowyn daye bake brede dele cryſten ſoules yet ben ſome vſen fewe ¶we fynde legenda aurea knyght ſhold goo batayle coſyn loued paſſyng well ſaid hym thus ſleyn batayle ſhold ſelle horſe deale valure pour people almeſſe praye criſten ſoules soo happed ſlayne coſyn loued well horſe toke hym owne vſe▪ thenne ſoone knyght appered coſyn ſaid thus hym thyſe viii dayes horſe thou haſte made brenne purgatory therfore god wyll take vengeaū ce forſothe quod daye thy ſoule ſhal helle wyth fende et ego purgatus vado ī regnū dei purged ſhal go kingedom heuen anone horryble noyſe herde thayre fendes caught man bare hym awaye thirde helpeth maſſe whan ony ſoule appereth ony man haue ony helpe deſyreth maſſes prayeth haue maſſes ſongē hym ryght mete drynke comforteth man whan feble ſo ſacramente awter comforteth ſoules maſſes ben done wreten legenda aurea biſhop ſuſpended preeſt cowde ſaye none maſſe requiem ſonge euery daye deuoutly connyng thenne daye byſſhop wente toward matens ſemed hym dede bodyes roſen rome bowte hym ſayde thou haſt ſaid noo maſſe v ouer thou haſt taken preſte away vs· loke amended ▪ elles god wyll ſhorte tyme take vengeaunce ſake thenne byſſhop gretely ferd anone bad preſt ſynge maſſe requyem▪ dyde fore ſoo dyde o ofte myghte ¶narracio ¶alſo fynde fiſſhers ſette nettes herueſt fyſſhe toke vp grete peſe yſe yt coldeſt yſe euer felte wolde melte ſonne thenne brought yſe byſſhop grete brennyg hete fote coldeſt euer felte thenne ſpake voys hym yſe ſayd ſoule ſuffre penaūce yſe haue noo frendes wyll doo maſſes ſhal delyuered penaunce thou ſhalt hole thy ſykeneſſe yf thou wylt ſaye maſſe ſaid wold ſinge hym bad telle hym name euer whyle maſſe layed yſe vnder fet euer ſaid maſſe yſe melte awaye ſoo wythin whyle yſe molten ſoule peyn byſſhop hole ſykeneſſe ¶thenne ſoule appered hym wyth moche ioye▪ ſayde wyth thy maſſes ſyngyng holpen oute peyne euerlaſtynge blyſſe tolde biſſhop ſhold deye ſoone come euerlaſtynge ioye wythout ende whiche god brynge v amen ¶de feſto ſctī ••• ī good frendis ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaynt marten daye whan marten xv yere age cutte mantell two peces rode amonge knyghtes yet cryſtened gaue halfe mantell poure man goddis ſake aſked almeſſe thenne nyghte god ſame clothe ſaid angel marten yet cryſtened hath clothed clothe marten herd worde oute heuen anone criſtened thenne anone lefte worldes occupacion gaue hym holyneſſe soo rode tyme waye fende come lykeneſſe man met hym aſked wheder wold ſayde thyder god wyll thenne ſaid fē de wyll thy ennemy thenne ſayd marten god helpe therfore drede thenne marten wexed ſo holy rered dede bodyes lyff ſoo grete holyneſſe choſen byſſhop turon tyme men grete perel lyke ſpilte one hē knew holyneſſe marten ſayde marten helpe anone holpē alſo rode tyme viſytacion hoūd ran hare vnder hors fete thenne pyte beſte bad hoūde ſtonde ſtyll lete beſt go anone hoūde ſtode ſtyl put erthe alſo ſawe adder ſwīmyng water ſaid thadder nomine dnī uibeo te redire name god cōmaūde goo ayen thou comeſt fro anone ſhe tourned ayen thenne marten ſighed wonder ſore ſaide ſory ſerpentes heren men wyll ¶a nother tyme come gate cyte hyght parys kyſſed horryble meſel anone hole ſame kyſſe alſo ſo pacient many tymes clerkes mocked hym yet ſuffred paciently wroth tyme rode waye viſytacion yt maner roughe mantell blacke came carte waye wyth caryage beſtes carte ſawe blacke waueryng wyth wynde fled awaye brake gere thenne carter wyth whyppe al bete marten gaue hym many ſore ſtrokes ſuffred mekely ſayd noo thyng thē wolde haue gone waye myght ſtere fro place tyll knowe yt marten thēne • ryed hym mercy thenne anone forgaue beſtes paſſed fai •• forth harneis ſauf ynough alſo tyme marten ſatt ſette fende come hym lykeneſſe kynge wyth ſhynynge crowne ſayd come fro heuē ſpeke wyth byleue criſtus ego ſum▪ cryſt marten loked hym ſaide lord iheſu cryſt wyll come ſuche araye thou criſt ſhew thy woū de anone fende went wai lefte horryble ſtenche behynde hym ¶yet another tyme come marten repreued hym toke people hym ſynned ſhreuen tourned ayen ſinne done fore ſayd though thou take grace god wil thenne ſayd marten wretche thou wyll leue purſute cryſten people aſke mercy wyth meke herte truſte god ſo mercyfull wyll gyue mercy whan marten ſhold paſſe oute world laye dede bed ▪ fende come ſatte hym dyſputynge wyth hym yf myghte haue caughte hym ony worde myſſe byleue ende marten ſayd hym goo hen thou cruell beeſte thou ſhall noo thynge fynde amyſſe wyth god ſhall receyue thenne made lay hym aſſhes heyre thenne ſayd ſeuen ſpſalmes letany gaue vp gooſt beryed owne chirche wyth moche honor thenne liiii wynters come biſſhop tranſlated hym whan made thynge redy layed honde marten body haue borne forthe myght thenne thoughte byſſhop marten wil remeued lefte thenne come fayre olde man bad hym go ayen wolde helpe hym thenne bare body tō wythout lettyng ſo whan ſeruyce done olde man
